<script>
  // Accessibility fix for Ask a Question button and modal on Yotpo
  window.addEventListener("load", function () {
    (function () {
      const focusTrap = (modal, triggerButton) => {
        const focusableSelectors =
          'a[href], area[href], input:not([disabled]), select:not([disabled]), textarea:not([disabled]), \
          button:not([disabled]), iframe, object, embed, [tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"]), [contenteditable]';
        const focusableElements = modal.querySelectorAll(focusableSelectors);
        if (!focusableElements.length) return;

        const firstEl = focusableElements[0];
        const lastEl = focusableElements[focusableElements.length - 1];

        const handleKeydown = (e) => {
          if (e.key === "Tab") {
            if (e.shiftKey) {
              if (document.activeElement === firstEl) {
                e.preventDefault();
                lastEl.focus();
              }
            } else {
              if (document.activeElement === lastEl) {
                e.preventDefault();
                firstEl.focus();
              }
            }
          }

          if (e.key === "Escape") {
            // Find and click the Yotpo close button to let Yotpo handle the closing
            const closeButton = modal.querySelector('.yotpo-close-icon');
            if (closeButton) {
              // Check if the SVG has a clickable parent
              const clickableParent = closeButton.closest('button, [role="button"], .yotpo-close');
              if (clickableParent && typeof clickableParent.click === 'function') {
                clickableParent.click();
              } else {
                // Dispatch a click event on the SVG element
                const clickEvent = new MouseEvent('click', {
                  bubbles: true,
                  cancelable: true,
                  view: window
                });
                closeButton.dispatchEvent(clickEvent);
              }
            } else {
              // Fallback: try to find any button that might close the modal
              const buttons = modal.querySelectorAll('button, [role="button"]');
              const possibleCloseButton = Array.from(buttons).find(btn => 
                btn.textContent.toLowerCase().includes('close') || 
                btn.textContent.toLowerCase().includes('cancel') ||
                btn.getAttribute('aria-label')?.toLowerCase().includes('close')
              );
              if (possibleCloseButton) {
                if (typeof possibleCloseButton.click === 'function') {
                  possibleCloseButton.click();
                } else {
                  // Dispatch click event for non-button elements
                  const clickEvent = new MouseEvent('click', {
                    bubbles: true,
                    cancelable: true,
                    view: window
                  });
                  possibleCloseButton.dispatchEvent(clickEvent);
                }
              }
            }
            document.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeydown);
            triggerButton?.focus(); // Return focus to the trigger button
          }
        };

        document.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeydown);
        firstEl.focus();
      };

      const handleYotpoModal = () => {
        const triggerButton = document.querySelector("#yotpo-widget-btn.yotpo-question-btn");
        if (!triggerButton) {
          return;
        }

        const activateModal = () => {
          const checkForModal = setInterval(() => {
            const modal = document.querySelector(".yotpo-qna-modal");
            if (modal && modal.offsetParent !== null) {
              clearInterval(checkForModal);

              modal.setAttribute("role", "dialog");
              modal.setAttribute("aria-modal", "true");
              modal.setAttribute("tabindex", "-1");

              // Trap focus once modal is ready
              setTimeout(() => focusTrap(modal, triggerButton), 100);
            }
          }, 100);
        };

        // Mouse click
        triggerButton.addEventListener("click", activateModal);

        // Keyboard interaction (Enter or Space)
        triggerButton.addEventListener("keydown", (e) => {
          if (e.key === "Enter" || e.key === " ") {
            e.preventDefault(); // Prevent scrolling on Space
            triggerButton.click(); // Triggers the same click handler
          }
        });
      };

      const waitForYotpo = setInterval(() => {
        const isProductPage = document.body.classList.contains("template-product");
        const yotpoLoaded = document.querySelector(".yotpo-widget-instance");

        if (isProductPage && yotpoLoaded) {
          clearInterval(waitForYotpo);
          console.log('Yotpo widget loaded on product page');
          handleYotpoModal();
        }
      }, 200);

      // Wait for the Q&A tab to be displayed
      const waitForTriggerButton = setInterval(() => {
        const triggerButton = document.querySelector("#yotpo-widget-btn.yotpo-question-btn");
        if (triggerButton) {
          clearInterval(waitForTriggerButton);
          console.log('Trigger button found');
          handleYotpoModal();
        }
      }, 200);
    })();
  });
</script>
